OPT(j) min-cost p₁,...,pⱼ ^sSXXPgj8

Lemma: ^giO1VudI

seek for i s.t. when appended character j, cost of new word formed splitting from i, ^ previous cost OPT(i-1) (previous word splits) is minimum ^vLPQJ0SZ

M[0]=0
for j=1,...,n:
    m=c₁ⱼ+M[0]
    for i=2,...,j:
        if cᵢⱼ+M[i-1]<m:
            m=cᵢⱼ+M[i-1]
    M[j]=m ^TRfm7guV
